  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_6735fcc2-9e2f-491f-9fd6-f37caebac1b9'
      });

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">I really really liked it a lot. Yes, even I crave for more Chloe and Bennett every single time, because let's face it: They are one of the best and ho<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">I really really liked it a lot. Yes, even I crave for more Chloe and Bennett every single time, because let's face it: They are one of the best and hottest couples I have ever read about. But Max and Sara also deserved a bit of the coverage and hence I felt it was justified.<br />But I would never object to the idea of getting at least three more books on Chloe and Bennett alone.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer598780952" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9914467425515360650"><b>*****3.5 Stars*****</b><br/><br/><br/><br/><a href='http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/360656d1a151830ae79287e194638f9f_zpsxduabl8l.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428260230i/14397029._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 360656d1a151830ae79287e194638f9f_zpsxduabl8l.jpg' width='365' height='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><br/>It's Valentine's Day weekend, and Bennett, his brother Henry, Max, and Will are all in Vegas for some Bachelor Party fun!! There will be some surprise guests, some sexy Champagne room escapades, and of course a couple of crazy shenanigans. Picture the movie, <b>"The Hangover"</b>, minus Mike Tyson, the tiger, and the baby!! <br/><br/><br/><br/><br/>There are several hot scenes between Bennett & Chloe, and Max & Sara, which having read most of the series you will come to expect there to be a lot of steam.</span>
  <span id="freeText9914467425515360650" style="display:none"><b>*****3.5 Stars*****</b><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s1276.photobucket.com/user/tennyspa/media/360656d1a151830ae79287e194638f9f_zpsxduabl8l.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428260230i/14397029._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 360656d1a151830ae79287e194638f9f_zpsxduabl8l.jpg" width="365" height="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><br>It's Valentine's Day weekend, and Bennett, his brother Henry, Max, and Will are all in Vegas for some Bachelor Party fun!! There will be some surprise guests, some sexy Champagne room escapades, and of course a couple of crazy shenanigans. Picture the movie, <b>"The Hangover"</b>, minus Mike Tyson, the tiger, and the baby!! <br><br><br><br><br>There are several hot scenes between Bennett &amp; Chloe, and Max &amp; Sara, which having read most of the series you will come to expect there to be a lot of steam. I found this to be an okay read and figured the purpose of this story was to let us spend more time with our favorite characters and to get an introduction to Mr Will Sumner. I read all the full length novels without having read any of the novellas. It didn't affect my love for books 1 through 3. However, if you need a quick and enjoyable in-between read this will do the trick.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9914467425515360650" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer665773486" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer7185353861155690297"><b>Viva Las Vegas! With Bastards and Strangers and Players, Oh My!</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387331260ra/7579304.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I'm a fan of this series, but I'll admit I started this book with low expectations. I wasn't exactly blown away by the last novella <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17831616.Beautiful_Bitch__Beautiful_Bastard___1_5_' title='Beautiful Bitch (Beautiful Bastard, #1.5) by Christina Lauren' rel='nofollow noopener'>Beautiful Bitch</a>… So I was pleasantly laughed-out-loud-several-times pleased with this! <br/><b>I grinned so much <i>my face hurt.</i></b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387331260ra/7579303.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Valentines Weekend. Bennett's Bachelor Party. Las Vegas.<br/>...But the girls decided not to stay home…</b><br/><br/>I loved watching Max and Bennett run all over Las Vegas like love-struck idiots... <br/><a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view </a></span>
  <span id="freeText7185353861155690297" style="display:none"><b>Viva Las Vegas! With Bastards and Strangers and Players, Oh My!</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387331260ra/7579304.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm a fan of this series, but I'll admit I started this book with low expectations. I wasn't exactly blown away by the last novella <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17831616.Beautiful_Bitch__Beautiful_Bastard___1_5_" title="Beautiful Bitch (Beautiful Bastard, #1.5) by Christina Lauren" rel="nofollow noopener">Beautiful Bitch</a>… So I was pleasantly laughed-out-loud-several-times pleased with this! <br><b>I grinned so much <i>my face hurt.</i></b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387331260ra/7579303.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Valentines Weekend. Bennett's Bachelor Party. Las Vegas.<br>...But the girls decided not to stay home…</b><br><br>I loved watching Max and Bennett run all over Las Vegas like love-struck idiots... <br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Sneaking away from the Bachelor Party to meet up with their girls... <br><b>Surprise private lap-dances, <br>voyeurism,<br>commandeering bathrooms, <br><s>stealing</s> <i>borrowing</i> limousines, <br>sexy moments in darkened peepshow theaters, <br>various pranks (some better accomplished than others), <br>lip-locks with high-class-cross-dressing prostitutes, <br>blackjack players with epic mustaches, <br>run-ins with testosterone-laden goons, <br>and enough scotch &amp; vodka to drown a moose!</b> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1387331260ra/7579305.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I liked that the usual dual POV was split this time between Bennett and Max. Yes, I understand that these novellas are basically just springboards for introducing a new character for the upcoming novels (looking at you Will). And no, I wasn't surprised by the twists this provided, but it was still a fun read!<br><br><br><b>
  <u>Some of My Favorite Moments</u>
</b><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387294376i/7570988.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>“You fucking wreck me, Chlo”<br><br>“Oh <i>God</i> . . .” Pulling her bottom lip into her mouth, she arched away and I bent to her neck, sucking, biting, <i>owning</i> her fucking heartbeat.<br>I felt the hammering of her pulse against my lips, felt each one of her exhales as she gasped, tensing above me and around me as she came. With a hoarse cry, she said my name and her voice sent a vibration across my tongue, pressed to her throat.<br><br>“What are you feeling?” I managed, lips pressed just below her ear. “Power? Control? Here you are, blindfolded and tied to a table and I’m fucking <i>lost</i> in you. I’m so fucking lost I can barely catch my breath.”<br><br>Will leaned back against the brick façade, hands in his pocket and suit jacket tucked in the crook of his arm. “So how are we continuing this weekend of debauchery? Dinner and then what? Skydiving? Virgin sacrifice? Matching tattoos to commemorate the loss of Ben’s balls?”<br><br>I relished knowing that she would always keep me guessing. Because of her wild independence, I would never know absolutely everything in her mind. Even when she was entirely <i>mine</i>, she would always be a challenge.<br><br>Seriously fucked-up situation we had going on here.<br><i>Still.</i><br><br>“Someone might see us,” she murmured, head falling back against the seat and eyes fluttering closed. She struggled to find words as I added a second finger, pushing them both in at once. I smiled at how breathless she was, how immediately incoherent.<br>“Isn’t that the point?”<br>“Cameras . . .”<br>I glanced up and shrugged. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387294376i/7570989.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>"Would you come on my hand as soon as you heard their feet on the stairs?”<br><br>“So how are the boys?”<br>“Replacing most of their blood with vodka and discussing the beauty of aged meats.”<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1387295513i/7571309.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>“You’re a bunch of assholes...<br>...But as far as kissing a dude went, that actually wasn’t bad.”<br><br>“This isn’t over. He’s going to bide his time, and then completely ruin us. Do you have any idea what I’ve done tonight to be with this woman? I snuck out on my best friend’s stag weekend. I stole a limousine. I hired my other best friend a drag queen, Bennett”<br><br>“They don’t even know you’re here, do they? Oh my God, they do. That’s why you’ve both been idiots all night. It’s like the four of you have subconscious homing devices implanted in your genitalia.”<br><br>...I had no choice but to fall for her; Sara was as irresistible as gravity.<br><br>Neither man was taller than me, but I had the distinct impression they had more hand-to-hand combat training than did I. Which is to say, some.<br><br><i>Fuck, she’s beautiful</i>, I thought, with her arms stretched over her head, her hands searching for the anchor the rest of her didn’t seem to feel.<br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><b>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1101813670" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer10401987673911323837">Another good novella from the <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16102004.Beautiful_Bastard__Beautiful_Bastard___1_' title='Beautiful Bastard (Beautiful Bastard, #1) by Christina Lauren' rel='nofollow noopener'>Beautiful Bastard</a> series. In addition to OG Bennett and Chloe, we also get to see how Max and Sara from <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16117506.Beautiful_Stranger__Beautiful_Bastard___2_' title='Beautiful Stranger (Beautiful Bastard, #2) by Christina Lauren' rel='nofollow noopener'>Beautiful Stranger</a> are doing. Though I’m <i>still</i> not a fan of theirs, they were less cringy in this book. And as always, William was adorable.</span>
  <span id="freeText10401987673911323837" style="display:none">Another good novella from the <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16102004.Beautiful_Bastard__Beautiful_Bastard___1_" title="Beautiful Bastard (Beautiful Bastard, #1) by Christina Lauren" rel="nofollow noopener">Beautiful Bastard</a> series. In addition to OG Bennett and Chloe, we also get to see how Max and Sara from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16117506.Beautiful_Stranger__Beautiful_Bastard___2_" title="Beautiful Stranger (Beautiful Bastard, #2) by Christina Lauren" rel="nofollow noopener">Beautiful Stranger</a> are doing. Though I’m <i>still</i> not a fan of theirs, they were less cringy in this book. And as always, William was adorable.</span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1354611399" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17963716520290104335">Rating: 3.5/5<br/><br/><b>Original review on <a href='http://julaliciousbookparadise.blogspot.ca/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Julalicious Book Paradise</a></b><br/><br/>So this novella was interesting, but I was not in love with it. I felt like they wanted to put so much stuff in the same book and it was really too much stuff for the length of this novella.<br/><br/>I felt that perhaps, they should have done a novella for Bennett and one for Max or just make it longer. Heck, I wouldn't mind 50-100 pages more if it meant like everything wasn't so confusing.<br/><br/>But I still liked it and I'm still glad that I read it becau</span>
  <span id="freeText17963716520290104335" style="display:none">Rating: 3.5/5<br /><br /><b>Original review on <a href="http://julaliciousbookparadise.blogspot.ca/" rel="nofollow noopener">Julalicious Book Paradise</a></b><br /><br />So this novella was interesting, but I was not in love with it. I felt like they wanted to put so much stuff in the same book and it was really too much stuff for the length of this novella.<br /><br />I felt that perhaps, they should have done a novella for Bennett and one for Max or just make it longer. Heck, I wouldn't mind 50-100 pages more if it meant like everything wasn't so confusing.<br /><br />But I still liked it and I'm still glad that I read it because it was funny and sexy too. So what happens in Vegas stays in Vegas? I don't know, but either way, it's a bachelor party that none of the guys are about to forget.<br /><br />Also, I was kind of bummed that Henry was there, but at the same time, not really. I felt like he popped from time to time. Even when he was there, I just felt like he was pushed out of the picture to talk more about Bennett, Max and Will.<br /><br />But if you read that series, it could be good to read the novellas to give you some insight that may explain certain things in the following books.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1686406136116968433">As much as I enjoy the full length books in this series, characters I like in long form don't do anything for me in these short vignettes. Both BEAUTIFUL BASTARD and BEAUTIFUL STRANGER had some of the most passionate sex scenes I've read in a long time, but those same characters going at it without story around them just seems like any other erotica short. Specific, graphic, and utterly forgettable. I can't wait to read Will's story, however, and will continue to look forward to this series' ful</span>
  <span id="freeText1686406136116968433" style="display:none">As much as I enjoy the full length books in this series, characters I like in long form don't do anything for me in these short vignettes. Both BEAUTIFUL BASTARD and BEAUTIFUL STRANGER had some of the most passionate sex scenes I've read in a long time, but those same characters going at it without story around them just seems like any other erotica short. Specific, graphic, and utterly forgettable. I can't wait to read Will's story, however, and will continue to look forward to this series' full length offerings.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13580712943629407750">*ARC Given to Blog for Honest Review*<br/><br/>4 <b> “fucking lost in you” </b> Kisses<br/><br/>Leave it to the Beautiful Bastard crew to do Vegas right. These little novellas do nothing but feeding my craving for wanting more of these absolutely insatiable characters. Well, I am rarely short and sweet…but that’s what <i> Beautiful Bombshell </i> gave me, so that’s what I will give to you.   <span id="freeText13580712943629407750" style="display:none">*ARC Given to Blog for Honest Review*<br><br>4 <b> “fucking lost in you” </b> Kisses<br><br>Leave it to the Beautiful Bastard crew to do Vegas right. These little novellas do nothing but feeding my craving for wanting more of these absolutely insatiable characters. Well, I am rarely short and sweet…but that’s what <i> Beautiful Bombshell </i> gave me, so that’s what I will give to you. Don’t get me wrong, it might have been short and sweet but it was hot, steamy, enticing and everything else I absolutely love about this series as well.<br><br>So the guys are in Vegas for Bennett’s <i>stag</i> weekend…what trouble can they really get into? Well…we don’t have to worry about that because the girls storm Vegas and take care of all the trouble you could possibly imagine. The whole thing is classic B.B. and I loved it. Every time I thought things might calm down, in typical B.B. fashion, all they did was push the envelope and continue to keep my eyebrow arched.<br><br><b> ‘My mind exploded with reactions: relief and anger, shock and embarrassment. Here Chloe was, in Vegas, not skiing in the fucking Catskills, and she’d come in here to find me blindfolded and waiting for a dancer to do exactly what she’d done: dance on my thighs, grind herself into my cock. But for once I’d managed to do with Chlose what I’d been able to do in every one of my business relationships: <i> hid the reaction you have until you’ve transformed it into the reaction you want.<i> ‘ </i></i></b><br><br>Max and Sara – I sincerely hope that they get their own novella’s too because these little tastes here and there, <b>especially</b> now with what we learn in <i>Beautiful Bombshell</i>, I am just as now invested in them as I am in Chloe and Bennett. I’m sorry – they’re fuckin’ hot and the exhibitionism level gets turned <i>way</i> up. If I didn’t love Sara, I’d cut a bitch cause Max Stella is to die for.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380435053ra/878674.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> ‘With a smile, I leaned in to kiss her, letting her deepen it with her hands on my face, sliding into my hair and around the back of my neck. “I feel like I could fuck for hours,” she whispered into my mouth and I almost lost it right then; Sara rarely swore, ad when she did, it always made me hard. “I just feel a little hollow with how much I want you tonight.”<br>I groaned and pressed my face into her neck.’ </b><br><br>And now….to the couple of the hour Bennett and Chloe. Oh boy. Wow…yeah, every book their connection grows deeper for me. I <b>l.o.v.e</b> them together. They’re hot, they’re passionate and they’re sensual. But it’s more than just the sex, it’s about the connection that they share and the emotions behind the sex that makes it more meaningful and more powerful. They’re just <b>hot!</b> The end. :-)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380435053i/878675.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I do have to say I missed not being in Chloe and Sara’s minds. I didn’t think I would because…well, Bennett and Max are just wonderful minds to be in – but I did. I missed their POV’s, especially with the encounters they were having and <i>especially</i> with Miss. Mills and all her…antics, I was sorry to miss her glorious thoughts. Chloe never fails to bring a smile to my face and give that added kick of excitement.<br><br><b> ‘“In fact, if you ever stop doing crazy things like that, stop being wild and foolish because you want me so much, it might just ruin me a little.”<br>“A little?” I could hear the smile in her voice.’ </b><br><br>Will…oh the precursors for Will’s book in <i>Beautiful Bombshell</i> were fab-u-lous to say the least. This book is the ultimate set up for <i>Beautiful Player</i> in my opinion and there is a piece of the prologue in the back of <i>Beautiful Bombshell</i> where we get to meet Hannah too. These two are going to be fun! Cannot wait for October 29th (<i>Beautiful Player</i>) and November 18th (<i>Beautiful Beginning</i>)! :-)<br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7782153838309317235"><b>Welcome to Vegas: The City of Sin!</b><br/><br/>OMG I <b>freakin’ loved</b> this novella! It was such a fun read! This novella was a mix of hilarious, sexy, adventure, sass, friendship, & drunkenness :D.<br/><br/>The relationship between the boys was such a kick. I seriously can’t get enough of their bromance! Oh and don’t even get me started on what these two did to get to their women hahaha; <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[stealing a limo, faking an ulcer & even hiring a woman (who turned out to a man) to distract Will :D <a class='jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction'>(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. A</span>
  <span id="freeText7782153838309317235" style="display:none"><b>Welcome to Vegas: The City of Sin!</b><br><br>OMG I <b>freakin’ loved</b> this novella! It was such a fun read! This novella was a mix of hilarious, sexy, adventure, sass, friendship, &amp; drunkenness :D.<br><br>The relationship between the boys was such a kick. I seriously can’t get enough of their bromance! Oh and don’t even get me started on what these two did to get to their women hahaha; <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[stealing a limo, faking an ulcer &amp; even hiring a woman (who turned out to a man) to distract Will :D <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. I would have loved for it to be longer *sigh*. Shit, it would be awesome if there was a book on just the guys &amp; their craziness lol. This was another great novella to the series &amp; it was definitely my favorite just simply because the boys made it so much fun &amp; there was whole lot of more sex than in ‘Beautiful Bitch’.<br><br><b>Will, I'm ready for you, baby!</b><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10117827583013593160"><b>Sexy and great fun! <br/><br/>4 stars</b><br/><br/>It’s Valentine’s Day, and Bennett has taken off to Las Vegas with Max, Will and Henry for his stag’s weekend. Of course that’s no fun, so Chloe and Sara sneak along to ensure that good times are had. <br/><br/>What follows is Bennett & Chloe, and Max & Sara’s sexcapades across Vegas as the boys keep making hilariously lame excuses to sneak off and have a little one-on-one time with their girls, followed by a bit of guys’ time with drinks and pranks galore as the night progresses</span>
  <span id="freeText10117827583013593160" style="display:none"><b>Sexy and great fun! <br /><br />4 stars</b><br /><br />It’s Valentine’s Day, and Bennett has taken off to Las Vegas with Max, Will and Henry for his stag’s weekend. Of course that’s no fun, so Chloe and Sara sneak along to ensure that good times are had. <br /><br />What follows is Bennett &amp; Chloe, and Max &amp; Sara’s sexcapades across Vegas as the boys keep making hilariously lame excuses to sneak off and have a little one-on-one time with their girls, followed by a bit of guys’ time with drinks and pranks galore as the night progresses<br /><br />It’s hot, it’s funny, and it’s just as much fun as I was expecting it to be. Not exactly a must-read, but if you’re a fan, you won’t want to miss out on a chance to catch up with this bunch – especially when they’re at their debauched best ;)<br /><br />I loved it! 4 stars.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('mCB/pcfD4TYFKqdVGVBmRB5hdM/Q8elRgX+X2yGUAotJAwexfKNu62YXj859mSAZF8G6Of4LAfzrkU9M8Gk98g==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('58sq7roOmbIy47NQYcc8JGODCLns4NR4JjjqBj6fby426FL6AW4Wb1Hem8sFDnp5aiPGT8IaPNVM1jKR72JQVw==')})
  }
